GT: c0*(c1 - P/c2)*P + c3*P**c4
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is a fixed function of **P only** (no dependence on *t*):
\[
0.953996983528\,(1-\tfrac{P}{96.9068829767})P\;+\;0.953996983528\,P^{1/3}
\]
So it is the sum of:
- a **quadratic polynomial in \(P\)**: \(aP - bP^2\) with \(a=0.953996983528\), \(b=0.953996983528/96.9068829767\neq 0\)
- plus a **fractional power term** \(0.953996983528\,P^{1/3}\).

Therefore any matching candidate must be able (by parameter choice) to produce **both** a nonzero \(P^2\) term, a nonzero \(P\) term, and a \(P^{1/3}\) term, and must have **no residual \(t\)-dependence** and no non-algebraic-in-\(P\) artifacts (logs, tanh, Max, Abs, rational pieces) that cannot be made identically equal to \(P^{1/3}\) for all \(P\).

Now check candidates:

1. Has logs in \(t\), Max, and log(P) products. You can zero out those terms, leaving only a quadratic polynomial \(c0P^2+c1P+c6\). No way to create \(P^{1/3}\). **No**.

2. Built from \(\frac{\text{polynomials in }P,\ |P|}{c1+|P|}\) plus tanh(t) pieces. Can kill tanh terms, but remaining is rational in \(|P|\), not \(P^{1/3}\) plus polynomial for all \(P\). **No**.

3. Polynomial + logs + Max + nested log. Can zero out nonpolynomial terms, leaving polynomial only; cannot get \(P^{1/3}\). **No**.

4. Polynomial + \(P\log(\cdot)\). Can remove log term; left polynomial only. **No**.

5. Polynomial + \(P|P|\) + rational + tanh(t). Even if kill tanh and rational and \(P|P|\), left polynomial only. No \(P^{1/3}\). **No**.

6. Has \(P^{c3} \cdot c4 \log(c5|P|+1)\). Even if set \(c3=1/3\), there is still a log factor; cannot make \(\log(c5|P|+1)\) a nonzero constant for all \(P\) (unless \(c5=0\) giving log(1)=0, which kills the whole term). So cannot produce \(P^{1/3}\) term. **No**.

Also no separate pure \(P^{1/3}\) term. **No**.

8. Has \(P*c1/(P+c2)\), \(t/(c5+t^2)\), Max. Can kill t and Max, but remaining has rational \(P/(P+c2)\) not present in GT and cannot equal \(P^{1/3}\). **No**.

9. Polynomial + tanh(t) + \((c6|P|+1)^{c7}\). You could try to make \((c6|P|+1)^{c7}\) equal \(P^{1/3}\), but dependence is on \(|P|\) and has +1 shift; impossible for all real \(P\). If \(c6=0\) it becomes constant. So no \(P^{1/3}\). **No**.

10. Polynomial + \(P\log(|P|)\) + tanh(t). Kill tanh and log term → polynomial only. **No**.

11. Polynomial + \(P\log(|P|)\) + tanh(t). Same issue. **No**.

But \(P*c3/(Pc4+1)\) cannot be made identically 0 unless \(c3=0\), in which case it vanishes (good). Then candidate reduces to \(P^2 c0 + P c2 + c6 P^{1/3}\). This matches GT’s structure exactly (quadratic + linear + \(P^{1/3}\)), with no constant term. We can set:
- \(c1=0\)
- \(c7=0\)

- \(c5=1/3\)
- \(c6=0.953996983528\)
- \(c2=0.953996983528\)
